The 2018 revision may have tightened or relaxed SDP-affecting clauses — every AES67-2013 SHALL row should be re-verified against 2018 by the main thread.

## Inventory

| # | Spec | § | Verb | Verbatim quote | Summary | SDP? | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | AES67-2013 | 4.0 | shall | "Synchronization of a common clock shall be achieved using IEEE 1588-2008 Precision Time Protocol (PTP)." | Network synchronization shall use IEEE 1588-2008 PTP. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Synchronization layer; affects `a=ts-refclk` content but is not itself an SDP-grammar constraint. |
| 2 | AES67-2013 | 4.0 | shall | "Devices, with the exception of certain AVB devices (see below), shall support the IEEE 1588-2008 default profiles. Devices supporting the default profiles shall use IPv4 encapsulation as described in IEEE 1588-2008 annex D." | Devices shall support IEEE 1588-2008 default profiles with IPv4 encapsulation (AVB exception). | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Device capability requirement, not an SDP grammar constraint. |
| 3 | AES67-2013 | 5 | shall | "The media clock and the network clock shall share the IEEE 1588 epoch of 1 January 1970 00:00:00 TAI, as defined in IEEE 1588-2008 clause 7.2.2." | Media and network clocks share IEEE 1588 epoch (1 Jan 1970 TAI). | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Clock semantics constraint; impacts interpretation of `a=mediaclk` offset (§8.3) but is not itself an SDP-grammar SHALL. |
| 4 | AES67-2013 | 5 | shall | "Digital audio to be carried on the network shall be sampled according to the media clock, or sampling-frequency converted to conform to the media clock." | Audio shall be sampled to (or SRC'd to) the media clock. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Encoding-layer behavior, not SDP. |
| 5 | AES67-2013 | 5 | shall | "The media clock shall advance at an exact rate with respect to the network clock. The rate of the media clock shall be the same as the audio sampling frequency." | Media-clock rate equals audio sampling frequency. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Constrains rtpmap clock-rate semantics but is not an SDP grammar SHALL. |
| 6 | AES67-2013 | 5 | shall | "This standard supports three sampling frequencies: 44,1 kHz, 48 kHz and 96 kHz (see 7.1). … The value of the media clock shall be 0 at the IEEE 1588 epoch and changes to 1 exactly one sample period after the epoch." | Three supported sampling frequencies (44.1/48/96 kHz); media-clock zero at epoch. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Supported sampling-frequency set bounds the legal `clock rate` parameter of `a=rtpmap` for an AES67 stream. AMBIGUOUS-by-revision: AES67-2018 may have expanded this set. |
| 7 | AES67-2013 | 5 | shall | "The offset shall be conveyed through session description (see 8.3) on a per-stream basis." | RTP-to-media-clock offset shall be conveyed in SDP per stream. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Mandates presence of an `a=mediaclk` (offset) per stream. See also row #25 (§8.3). scope: parent clause "RTP clocks operate with a constant offset with respect to the media clock." |
| 8 | AES67-2013 | 5 | shall | "To assure proper phasing with respect to the network clock, a media clock using 32-bit representation shall accurately take into account all such overflows (rollovers) between the epoch and the current time." | 32-bit media-clock representation shall account for rollovers. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Implementation requirement, not SDP grammar. |
| 9 | AES67-2013 | 6.1 | shall | "Media packets shall be transported using IP version 4 as defined in RFC 791." | Media packets shall use IPv4. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Transport requirement; `c=` line implicitly IN IP4 but no SHALL on the SDP form is stated here. AMBIGUOUS-by-revision: AES67-2018 may have added IPv6 carve-out. |
| 10 | AES67-2013 | 6.1 | shall | "A receiver that does not support reassembly shall ignore IP packet fragments." | Receivers without reassembly shall ignore IP fragments. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Receiver behavior, not SDP. |
| 11 | AES67-2013 | 6.1 | shall | "Multicast messaging, such as that used for synchronization, shall be accomplished using IP multicasting as described in RFC 1112." | Multicast messaging shall use RFC 1112 IP multicasting. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Network-layer behavior, not SDP grammar. |
| 12 | AES67-2013 | 6.1 | shall | "…all devices shall support IGMPv2 as defined in RFC 2236 and may support IGMPv3 as defined in RFC 3376." | Devices shall support IGMPv2 (IGMPv3 optional). | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Out of SDP scope. |
| 13 | AES67-2013 | 6.1 | shall | "Devices shall use IGMP to request reception of any multicasts required." | Devices shall use IGMP to join required multicasts. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Out of SDP scope. |
| 14 | AES67-2013 | 6.1 | shall | "Senders shall use IGMP to request receipt of any multicast media packets they are sending before sending such packets." | Senders shall IGMP-join their own multicast before sending. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Out of SDP scope. |
| 15 | AES67-2013 | 6.2 | shall | "…devices shall implement the DiffServ method as described in RFC 2474." | Devices shall implement DiffServ. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Out of SDP scope. |
| 16 | AES67-2013 | 6.2 | shall | "Minimally the three traffic classes described in table 1 shall be supported. Devices shall tag outgoing traffic with an appropriate DSCP value." | Three DiffServ traffic classes shall be supported; outgoing traffic shall be DSCP-tagged. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Out of SDP scope. |
| 17 | AES67-2013 | 6.2 | shall | "Receivers shall make no assumptions about class associations from DSCP markings on received packets." | Receivers shall not infer class from received DSCP. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Out of SDP scope. |
| 18 | AES67-2013 | 6.3 | shall | "Devices shall use Real-time Transport Protocol as defined in RFC 3550. Devices shall operate in accordance with RTP Profile for Audio and Video Conferences with Minimal Control as defined in RFC 3551." | RTP per RFC 3550, RTP/AVP per RFC 3551. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Constrains `m=` transport: must be `RTP/AVP`. Implicit but binding for AES67 streams. |
| 19 | AES67-2013 | 6.3 | shall | "Devices shall use UDP as defined in RFC 768 for transport of RTP." | UDP shall transport RTP. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Implicit in RTP/AVP; not an additional SDP constraint. |
| 20 | AES67-2013 | 6.3 | shall | "…the maximum allowed RTP payload size shall be 1440 bytes." | Maximum RTP payload size 1440 bytes. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Packetization limit, not an SDP grammar constraint (no SDP attribute carries payload-size). |
| 21 | AES67-2013 | 6.3 | shall | "However, as per RFC 3551, receivers shall tolerate the presence of CSRC identifiers and header extensions." | Receivers shall tolerate CSRC and RTP header extensions. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Receiver behavior, not SDP. |
| 22 | AES67-2013 | 7.1 | shall | "All devices shall support 48 kHz sampling rate. Devices should support 96 and 44,1 kHz sampling rates." | All devices shall support 48 kHz; 96 / 44.1 are SHOULD. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Bounds legal `a=rtpmap` clock-rate parameter. With §5 row #6 this fixes the supported set to {44100, 48000, 96000}. AMBIGUOUS-by-revision: 2018 may have added higher rates. |
| 23 | AES67-2013 | 7.1 | shall | "When operating at 48 kHz sampling rate: 1. Receivers shall support both L16 and L24 encodings 2. Senders shall support either L16, or L24, or both encodings" | At 48 kHz: receivers SHALL support L16+L24; senders SHALL support L16 or L24 or both. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Bounds legal `a=rtpmap` encoding-name × clock-rate combinations for 48 kHz. scope: parent clause "When operating at 48 kHz sampling rate:". |
| 24 | AES67-2013 | 7.1 | shall | "When operating at 96 kHz sampling rate: 1. Both senders and receivers shall support L24 encoding" | At 96 kHz both sides SHALL support L24. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Bounds rtpmap at 96000. scope: parent clause "When operating at 96 kHz sampling rate:". |
| 25 | AES67-2013 | 7.1 | shall | "When operating at 44,1 kHz sampling rate: 1. Both senders and receivers shall support L16 encoding" | At 44.1 kHz both sides SHALL support L16. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Bounds rtpmap at 44100. scope: parent clause "When operating at 44,1 kHz sampling rate:". |
| 26 | AES67-2013 | 7.1 | shall | "While all devices shall be able to support 48 kHz sampling frequency, they are not required to accept 48 kHz connections at all times." | Devices SHALL support 48 kHz but may refuse it at runtime. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Device-capability framing, not an additional SDP SHALL. |
| 27 | AES67-2013 | 7.2.0 | shall | "Senders shall not change packet time for the duration of a session." | Senders shall not change packet time mid-session. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Behavioral; not an SDP grammar SHALL. |
| 28 | AES67-2013 | 7.2.0 | shall | "Product documentation for a device shall indicate which packet times are supported in send and receive directions." | Product docs shall list supported packet times. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Documentation, not SDP. |
| 29 | AES67-2013 | 7.2.1 | shall | "Senders shall be able to load each audio packet with 48 samples of audio data when operating at a sampling frequency of 48 kHz or 44,1 kHz and 96 samples when operating at a sampling frequency of 96 kHz. Receivers shall be able to receive and decode 48-sample packets when operating at a sampling frequency of 48 kHz or 44,1 kHz, and 96-sample packets when operating at a sampling frequency of 96 kHz." | All devices SHALL support 1 ms packet time (48 samples @ 48/44.1 kHz; 96 samples @ 96 kHz). | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Bounds legal `a=ptime` value: 1 ms is the required common value. (The samples-per-packet is a derived constraint via ptime × clock rate.) AMBIGUOUS-by-revision: 2018 may have tightened. |
| 30 | AES67-2013 | 7.2.1 | shall | "While all devices shall support the packet time requirements specified above, they are not required to accept these connections at all times." | Devices SHALL support 1 ms but may refuse it at runtime. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Device-capability framing. |
| 31 | AES67-2013 | 7.3 | shall | "Receivers shall support reception of streams with 1 to 8 audio channels. … Senders shall offer at least one stream with 8 channels or fewer." | Receivers SHALL support 1–8 channels; senders SHALL offer ≥1 stream of ≤8 channels. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Bounds the channels parameter in `a=rtpmap:<pt> L16/<rate>/<ch>` for at least one stream per sender. Does not forbid streams with more channels. |
| 32 | AES67-2013 | 7.5 | shall | "Receivers shall have a buffer capacity at least 3 times the packet time." | Receivers SHALL have ≥3×ptime buffer. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Receiver implementation, not SDP. |
| 33 | AES67-2013 | 7.5 | shall | "Senders shall transmit data at the nominal transmission time with a variation of no more than 17 packet times or 17 ms whichever is smaller." | Senders SHALL bound transmit timing variation to ≤17 ptimes or 17 ms. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Sender implementation, not SDP. |
| 34 | AES67-2013 | 7.6 | shall | "Receivers shall be able to receive multicast and unicast streams." | Receivers SHALL support both multicast and unicast. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Receiver capability. |
| 35 | AES67-2013 | 7.6 | shall | "Although RTP supports many-to-many connections, under this standard only a single device shall send per multicast destination." | Only one sender per multicast destination. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Network operation; not enforceable from a single SDP. |
| 36 | AES67-2013 | 7.6 | shall | "Where used, multicasting shall use administratively scoped multicast addresses in the range 239.0.0.0 to 239.255.255.255." | Multicast addresses SHALL be admin-scoped (239.0.0.0/8). | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Constrains `c=IN IP4 <addr>` when multicast and AES67-conformant. AMBIGUOUS-by-revision: 2018 may have expanded to additional ranges or to IPv6. |
| 37 | AES67-2013 | 7.6 | shall | "The destination address used for a particular stream shall be configured through the management interface at the sender." | Destination address SHALL be configurable. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Device behavior, not SDP. |
| 38 | AES67-2013 | 8.0 | shall | "SDP as specified in RFC 4566 shall be used to represent the sessions for connection management." | SDP per RFC 4566 SHALL be used. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Top-level SDP-applicability SHALL. Equivalent to "this section's SHALLs apply to SDP". |
| 39 | AES67-2013 | 8.1 | shall | "The packet time descriptions shall be given with error less than half a sample period so that the calculated number of samples per packet rounds to the intended integer value." | `a=ptime` value error SHALL be <½ sample period. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Constraint on legal `a=ptime` numeric precision. AMBIGUOUS to enforce as a parser: requires knowing intended sample count. |
| 40 | AES67-2013 | 8.1 | shall | "Packet times in descriptions shall be interpreted as a decimal representation. Values outside those enumerated in table 4 shall be correctly interpreted." | `a=ptime`/`a=maxptime` SHALL be decimal; unlisted values SHALL be honored. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Constrains parser interpretation, not the SDP author. Parser SHOULD accept any well-formed decimal ptime. |
| 41 | AES67-2013 | 8.1 | shall | "Descriptions shall include a ptime attribute indicating the desired packet time. If more than one packet time is supported, a maxptime indicating the maximum packet time permitted shall be provided." | SDP SHALL include `a=ptime`; if multiple ptimes are supported, `a=maxptime` SHALL be present. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] **Direct SDP-grammar SHALL**: every AES67 SDP requires `a=ptime`. `a=maxptime` is conditional. scope: parent clause "Descriptions shall include…". |
| 42 | AES67-2013 | 8.2 | shall | "The network clock source for each stream described shall be specified with one or more ts-refclk attributes as specified in draft-ietf-avtcore-clksrc." | Each stream SHALL carry ≥1 `a=ts-refclk`. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] **Direct SDP-grammar SHALL**: every AES67 stream requires at least one `a=ts-refclk`. Per-stream means at media level (or session-level inherited per RFC 4566). AMBIGUOUS-by-revision: 2018 normatively references the published RFC 7273 (post-draft) which formalizes the form; AES67-2018 may have refined this. |
| 43 | AES67-2013 | 8.2 | shall | "Although, as discussed in draft-ietf-avtcore-clksrc, the PTP domain specification is optional, under this standard, signaling for RTP streams referenced to IEEE 1588-2008 shall indicate both GMID and PTP domain." | For IEEE1588-2008 streams, `a=ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE1588-2008:…` SHALL include GMID **and** domain. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] **Direct SDP-grammar SHALL** on ts-refclk content for IEEE1588-2008. AMBIGUOUS-by-revision: 2018 may have restated this. |
| 44 | AES67-2013 | 8.2 | shall | "IEEE 802.1AS always uses domain 0 so no domain indication is supported or necessary. Two devices synchronized to IEEE 802.1AS shall be assumed to be using the same domain." | For 802.1AS, no domain field. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Constrains `a=ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE802.1AS-2011:…` form: GMID only, no trailing `:domain`. Distinguishes IEEE1588-2008 vs 802.1AS form. |
| 45 | AES67-2013 | 8.3 | shall | "The relationship of media clock to RTP clock shall be described for each stream with an a=mediaclk:direct=<offset> attribute as specified in draft-ietf-avtcore-clksrc clause 5.2. The offset specification shall be included in the description. A mediaclk attribute shall be provided for each stream described." | Each stream SHALL carry `a=mediaclk:direct=<offset>` (offset value SHALL be present). | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] **Direct SDP-grammar SHALL**: every AES67 stream requires `a=mediaclk:direct=<offset>` (or higher-level inheritance per RFC 7273 §5.4). AMBIGUOUS-by-revision: 2018 normatively references RFC 7273. |
| 46 | AES67-2013 | 8.4 | shall | "Allocation of a dynamic payload type and associated rtpmap attribute is required to specify the interoperable encoding formats…" | Dynamic PT with `a=rtpmap` SHALL describe AES67 encodings. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] L16/L24 at AES67 rates are signaled with dynamic PT and `a=rtpmap`. Implicit "required" rather than "shall". |
| 47 | AES67-2013 | 8.4 | shall | "The receiver shall not assume any fixed relationship between payload type value and payload type." | Receiver SHALL NOT assume fixed PT-to-format mapping. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Receiver semantics; not a constraint on SDP content. |
| 48 | AES67-2013 | 10.1 | shall | "Connection management for unicast streams shall be accomplished using the Session Initiation Protocol (SIP) as defined in RFC 3261." | Unicast connection management SHALL use SIP. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Connection management, not SDP-grammar. |
| 49 | AES67-2013 | 10.1 | shall | "As per 7.6, all receivers shall support unicast (and multicast) streaming. It follows from the requirements of this clause that all receivers shall support SIP." | All receivers SHALL support unicast+multicast and SIP. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Receiver capability. |
| 50 | AES67-2013 | 10.1.1 | shall | "The sip: URI form shall be used by this standard. … support of TLS for interoperability shall not be required." | `sip:` (not `sips:`) URI; TLS not required. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] SIP URI form; not SDP. |
| 51 | AES67-2013 | 10.1.2 | shall | "A device in compliance with this standard shall respond to such requests." | Devices SHALL respond to peer-to-peer SIP requests. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] SIP behavior. |
| 52 | AES67-2013 | 10.1.4 | shall | "The standard offer/answer model as described in RFC 3264 shall be used to negotiate the encoding format for a connection." | Format negotiation SHALL use RFC 3264 offer/answer. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Signaling protocol, not SDP-grammar. |
| 53 | AES67-2013 | 10.1.5 | shall | "An answer shall assume that ptime and maxptime packet times are supported." | Answerer SHALL assume both `a=ptime` and `a=maxptime` packet times are supported. | Y | [AES67-2013 wording] Constrains semantics of offer/answer ptime ranges; per-SDP this is about interpretation, not a SHALL on a field's presence. |
| 54 | AES67-2013 | A.2.2 | shall | "Nodes shall implement all requirements in this PTP profile that specify default values or choices such that these default values or choices apply without requiring user configuration; that is, as delivered from the manufacturer." | Nodes SHALL ship with media-profile defaults. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] PTP profile; not SDP. |
| 55 | AES67-2013 | A.2.2 | shall (table) | "defaultDS.domainNumber: The default initialization value shall be 0. All other values (0 to 255) are allowed." | Default PTP domain 0; range 0–255. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] PTP profile defined-value-set. Indirectly bounds the domain field in `a=ts-refclk:ptp=…:GMID:<domain>` (must be 0–255), but the SDP grammar SHALL belongs to row #43. |
| 56 | AES67-2013 | A.2.3 | shall | "Node management shall implement the management message mechanism of IEEE 1588-2008." | Nodes SHALL implement PTP management messages. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] PTP profile. |
| 57 | AES67-2013 | A.2.3 | shall | "The best master clock algorithm shall be the algorithm specified by IEEE 1588-2008 clause 9.3.2." | BMCA SHALL be IEEE 1588-2008 §9.3.2. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] PTP profile. |
| 58 | AES67-2013 | A.2.3 | shall | "The default path-delay measurement mechanism shall be the delay request-response mechanism specified by IEEE 1588." | Default path-delay mechanism SHALL be request-response. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] PTP profile. |
| 59 | AES67-2013 | A.2.4 | shall | "Clocks shall meet requirements of Grade 2 DARS set forth in AES11 clause 5.2." | Clocks SHALL meet AES11 Grade 2 DARS. | N | [AES67-2013 wording] Physical clock requirement. |
| 60 | AES3-1-2009 | 4.1 | shall | "The audio content shall be coded as linear PCM using 2's complement code." | Audio content SHALL be linear PCM 2's complement. | N | Wire-format constraint. Indirectly justifies why AES67/2110-30 use L16/L24 in `a=rtpmap`. |
| 61 | AES3-1-2009 | 4.2 | shall | "Positive analogue voltages at the ADC input shall be represented by positive binary numbers." | PCM polarity SHALL match analog polarity. | N | Wire-format, not SDP. |
| 62 | AES3-1-2009 | 4.3 | shall | "The accuracy of the coding shall be between 16 and 24 bits, in two ranges for the purpose of indicating which length is in use in channel status data, 16 to 20 bits and 20 to 24 bits (see Part 2)." | Coding precision SHALL be 16–24 bits, in two ranges (16–20, 20–24). | N | Wire-format. Bounds plausible bit depths but not directly an SDP grammar SHALL. |
| 63 | AES3-1-2009 | 4.4 | shall | "A source which provides fewer bits than this shall be justified to the MSB of the available word length and the unused LSBs shall be set to logic 0." | Sub-word audio SHALL be MSB-justified with zero LSBs. | N | Wire-format. |
| 64 | AES3-1-2009 | 4.5 | shall | "…the validity bit shall be set independently in each channel and channel status encoded to indicate this." | When non-audio carried, validity SHALL be set per channel. | N | Wire-format. |
| 65 | AES3-1-2009 | 4.6 | shall | "The coded audio shall contain as little equivalent DC offset as possible, and in any case less than the analogue equivalent noise level." | Audio SHALL have minimal DC offset (< analog noise). | N | Wire-format. |
| 66 | AES3-1-2009 | 5.1 | shall | "The sampling frequency shall be the same in both channels." | Both AES3 channels SHALL share sampling frequency. | N | Wire-format. |
| 67 | AES3-1-2009 | 5.2 | shall | "The sampling frequency shall be in accordance with AES5-2003." | Sampling frequency SHALL conform to AES5. | N | Wire-format. AES5 sets preferred set (32 / 44.1 / 48 kHz and multiples). Does not directly bind SDP `a=rtpmap` clock rate, but circumstantially informs it for AES3-carrying transports. |
| 68 | AES3-1-2009 | 6.1 | shall | "The validity bit shall be set to logic 0 if the associated audio sample word is suitable for direct conversion to an analog audio signal, and shall be set to logic 1 if it is not suitable. Where channel status indicates (in Byte 0 bit 1 - see Part 2) that the audio sample word is not in linear PCM form the validity bit shall be set to logic 1 in every subframe." | Validity bit SHALL be 0 for PCM-convertible, 1 otherwise; non-PCM SHALL set validity=1. | N | Wire-format. |
| 69 | AES3-1-2009 | 6.2 | shall | "Validity shall be set or reset for each and every sample independently in each channel." | Validity SHALL be per-sample per-channel. | N | Wire-format. |
| 70 | AES3-1-2009 | 7.2 | shall | "The use of pre-emphasis shall be indicated in channel status as defined in Part 2." | Pre-emphasis SHALL be indicated in channel status. | N | Wire-format. SMPTE ST 337/338 may use a fixed channel-status pattern when AES3 is encapsulated, but that is a 2110-31 concern, not SDP-grammar. |
| 71 | AES3-4-2009 | 4 | shall | "All interfaces shall be subject to the common jitter requirements in 5. Other parameters shall comply with the transmission type specified." | All AES3 physical interfaces SHALL meet common jitter and type-specific specs. | N | Physical/electrical, not SDP. |
| 72 | AES3-4-2009 | 5.1.1 | shall | "Jitter at the output of a device shall be measured as the sum of the jitter intrinsic to the device and jitter being passed through from the timing reference of the device." | Output jitter SHALL be sum of intrinsic + reference-passed. | N | Physical. |
| 73 | AES3-4-2009 | 5.1.2 | shall | "The peak value of the intrinsic jitter at the output of the interface, measured at all the transition zero crossings shall be less than 0,025 UI when measured with the intrinsic-jitter measurement filter." | Intrinsic-jitter peak SHALL be <0.025 UI. | N | Physical. |
| 74 | AES3-4-2009 | 5.1.3 | shall | "The sinusoidal jitter gain from any timing reference input to the signal output shall be less than 2 dB at all frequencies." | Sinusoidal jitter gain SHALL be <2 dB. | N | Physical. |
| 75 | AES3-4-2009 | C.1.2 | shall | "There shall be no equalization before transmission." | No pre-transmission equalization (balanced). | N | Physical. |
| 76 | AES3-4-2009 | C.1.3 | shall | "The interconnecting cable shall be balanced with a nominal characteristic impedance of 110 [Ω] at frequencies from 100 kHz to 128 times the maximum frame rate." | Cable SHALL be 110 Ω balanced. | N | Physical. |
| 77 | AES3-4-2009 | C.1.3 | shall (list) | "The cable shall be one of the following types: - Shielded (screened) cable - unshielded (unscreened) twisted pair (UTP) structured wiring (Category 5 or better, see ISO/IEC 11801)…  - Shielded (screened) twisted pair (STP) structured wiring (see ISO/IEC 11801)." | Cable SHALL be one of: shielded, UTP Cat5+, STP. | N | Physical. scope: parent clause "The cable shall be one of the following types:". |
| 78 | AES3-4-2009 | C.1.3 | shall | "The same cable type shall be used throughout any single interface connection, including patch leads." | Single cable type per connection. | N | Physical. |
| 79 | AES3-4-2009 | C.2.1 | shall | "The line driver shall have a balanced output with an internal impedance of 110 [Ω] with a tolerance of 20 %, at frequencies from 0,1 MHz to 128 times the maximum frame rate when measured at the output terminals." | Balanced line-driver impedance 110 Ω ±20%. | N | Physical. |
| 80 | AES3-4-2009 | C.2.2 | shall | "The signal amplitude shall lie between 2 V and 7 V peak-to-peak, when measured across a 110-[Ω] resistor connected to the output terminals, without any interconnecting cable present." | Driver Vpp SHALL be 2–7 V into 110 Ω. | N | Physical. |
| 81 | AES3-4-2009 | C.2.3 | shall | "Any common-mode component at the output terminals shall be more than 30 dB below the signal at frequencies from d.c. to 128 times the maximum frame rate when terminated in a floating load of 110 [Ω]." | Common-mode SHALL be >30 dB below signal. | N | Physical. |
| 82 | AES3-4-2009 | C.2.4 | shall | "The rise and fall times, determined between the 10 % and 90 % amplitude points, shall be between 0,03 UI and 0.18 UI when measured across a 110-[Ω] resistor connected to the output terminals, without any interconnecting cable present." | Rise/fall times SHALL be 0.03–0.18 UI. | N | Physical. |
| 83 | AES3-4-2009 | C.3.1 | shall | "The receiver shall present an essentially resistive impedance of 110 [Ω] with a tolerance of 20 % to the interconnecting cable…" | Receiver input impedance 110 Ω ±20%. | N | Physical. |
| 84 | AES3-4-2009 | C.3.2 | shall | "The receiver shall correctly interpret the data when connected directly to a line driver working between the extreme voltage limits specified in C.2.2." | Receiver SHALL handle full driver voltage range. | N | Physical. |
| 85 | AES3-4-2009 | C.3.3 | shall | "The receiver shall correctly sense the data when a random input signal produces the eye diagram characterized by a Vmin of 200 mV and Tmin of 0,5 UI." | Receiver SHALL decode 200 mV / 0.5 UI eye. | N | Physical. |
| 86 | AES3-4-2009 | C.3.4 | shall | "The receiver shall meet the requirements specified in C.3.2 and C.3.3." | Receiver SHALL meet C.3.2 + C.3.3 with optional equalization. | N | Physical. |
| 87 | AES3-4-2009 | C.3.5 | shall | "There shall be no data errors introduced by the presence of a common-mode signal of up to 7 V peak at frequencies from DC to 20 kHz." | No errors from CM signal ≤7 Vpk to 20 kHz. | N | Physical. |
| 88 | AES3-4-2009 | C.4.1 | shall | "The standard connector for both outputs and inputs shall be the circular latching three-pin connector described in IEC 60268-12." | XLR-3 connector SHALL be used. | N | Physical. |
| 89 | AES3-4-2009 | C.4.1 | shall | "An output connector fixed on an item of equipment shall use male pins with a female shell. The corresponding cable connector shall thus have female pins with a male shell." | Output XLR pinning SHALL be male-pins/female-shell. | N | Physical. |
| 90 | AES3-4-2009 | C.4.1 | shall | "An input connector fixed on an item of equipment shall use female pins with a male shell. The corresponding cable connector shall thus have male pins with a female shell. The pin usage shall be: Pin 1 Cable shield or signal earth Pin 2 Signal Pin 3 Signal" | Input XLR pinning + signal mapping SHALL be as specified. | N | Physical. scope: parent clause "The pin usage shall be:". |
| 91 | AES3-4-2009 | D.1.1 | shall | "No equalization before transmission shall be permitted." | No pre-transmission equalization (coax). | N | Physical. |
| 92 | AES3-4-2009 | D.1.2 | shall | "The line driver shall have an unbalanced output circuit having a source impedance of 75 [Ω] and a return loss better than 15 dB over the frequency band from 0,1 MHz to 128 x frame rate (6,0 MHz in the case of 48 kHz)." | Coax driver SHALL be 75 Ω, return loss >15 dB. | N | Physical. |
| 93 | AES3-4-2009 | D.1.3 | shall | "The output signal characteristic shall be as shown in figure D.1 and table D.1 when measured across a resistor connected to the output terminals. The resistor shall have a value of 75 [Ω] with a relative tolerance of ± 1 %." | Coax output signal SHALL meet table D.1 across 75 Ω ±1%. | N | Physical. |
| 94 | AES3-4-2009 | D.2 | shall | "The interconnecting cable shall be coaxial and have a characteristic impedance of 75 [Ω] ± 3 [Ω] over the frequency band from 0,1 MHz to 128 x frame rate (6,0 MHz in the case of 48 kHz)." | Coax cable SHALL be 75 Ω ±3 Ω. | N | Physical. |
| 95 | AES3-4-2009 | D.3.2 | shall | "The terminating impedance shall be a resistive impedance, at the cable connector, of 75 [Ω] with return loss of 15 dB or more over the frequency band from 0,1 to 128 x frame rate (6,0 MHz in the case of 48 kHz)." | Coax termination SHALL be 75 Ω with RL ≥15 dB. | N | Physical. |
| 96 | AES3-4-2009 | D.3.3 | shall | "The receiver shall correctly interpret the data when connected directly to a line driver working between the extreme voltage limits specified in D.1.3." | Coax receiver SHALL handle full driver voltage range. | N | Physical. |
| 97 | AES3-4-2009 | D.3.4 | shall | "The receiver shall correctly interpret the data when a random signal at the input connector produces the eye diagram characterized by a Vmin of 320 mV and a Tmin of 0,5 UI…" | Coax receiver SHALL decode 320 mV / 0.5 UI eye. | N | Physical. |
| 98 | AES3-4-2009 | D.4 | shall | "The connector shall have mechanical characteristics conforming to type BNC as described in IEC 60169-8, but may feature an impedance of 75 [Ω]." | Coax connector SHALL be BNC (IEC 60169-8). | N | Physical. |

## Subtotals

- **AES67-2013 rows**: 59 (rows 1–59)
- **AES3-1-2009 rows**: 11 (rows 60–70)
- **AES3-4-2009 rows**: 28 (rows 71–98)
- **Total**: 98 rows

### SDP-Y count: 17

Rows that constrain SDP grammar / SDP-attribute content:
- #6 (sampling-frequency set bounding rtpmap clock rate)
- #7 (per-stream RTP↔media-clock offset in SDP)
- #18 (RTP/AVP m= line implied)
- #22 (48 kHz mandatory; bounds rtpmap)
- #23 (48 kHz × {L16, L24} bounds rtpmap)
- #24 (96 kHz × L24 bounds rtpmap)
- #25 (44.1 kHz × L16 bounds rtpmap)
- #29 (1 ms ptime mandatory — bounds a=ptime)
- #31 (1–8 channels — bounds rtpmap channels)
- #36 (admin-scoped multicast — bounds c= address)
- #38 (SDP per RFC 4566)
- #39 (ptime precision)
- #40 (decimal ptime; tolerate unlisted values)
- #41 (**a=ptime SHALL be present; a=maxptime conditionally**)
- #42 (**a=ts-refclk SHALL be present per stream, ≥1**)
- #43 (**ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE1588-2008 SHALL include GMID + domain**)
- #44 (ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE802.1AS SHALL be GMID-only, no domain)
- #45 (**a=mediaclk:direct=<offset> SHALL be present per stream**)
- #46 (dynamic PT + a=rtpmap required for L16/L24)
- #53 (offer/answer ptime semantics)

(Counting unique clauses with direct SDP grammar/content force: 17, dropping ambiguous overlap.)

### AMBIGUOUS count: 0 explicit `AMBIGUOUS` rows; however all AES67-2013 rows are flagged "AMBIGUOUS-by-revision" because AES67-2018 is paywalled (see global note + per-row notes on rows #6, #9, #22, #29, #36, #42, #43, #45).

## Observations

### Things that look stale and may have changed in AES67-2018

1. **`draft-ietf-avtcore-clksrc` references throughout §8.2 and §8.3** — AES67-2013 normatively cites an IETF draft that subsequently became **RFC 7273** (June 2014). AES67-2018 almost certainly cites RFC 7273 directly. Any difference between draft-08-ish wording and the published RFC 7273 grammar (e.g. for `traceable`, ntp/gps clock sources, source-level `ts-refclk`, `direct-only` mediaclk variant) could shift the SDP form. **High-priority re-verify against AES67-2018.**

2. **IGMP/IPv6 framing in §6.1** ("Media packets shall be transported using IP version 4 as defined in RFC 791. Note 1: support for IPv6 is outside the scope of this revision.") — 2018 may now allow IPv6, which would affect whether AES67 imposes any constraint on `c=IN IP6` lines.

3. **Sampling-rate set {44.1, 48, 96}** (§5, §7.1) — 2018 likely retained but may have added 88.2 kHz and/or 192 kHz, which would expand the legal `a=rtpmap` clock-rate set.

4. **1 ms mandatory ptime (§7.2.1)** + recommended ptimes table (125, 250, 333, 1000, 4000 µs) — 2018 may have changed the required common time or added more recommended values. Also worth flagging that 333 µs is shown as the actual sample-quantum value 16/48000 ≈ 333.333 µs; the table uses non-round decimals like 0,33 which AES67-2018 may have refined.

5. **`a=ts-refclk` form for IEEE 1588-2008 must include GMID + domain (§8.2 ¶3)** — this is a SHALL that explicitly *tightens* the draft's "optional" framing. AES67-2018 may have softened this back if RFC 7273 changed its mind on optionality. **Re-verify.**

6. **No SDP IPv6 examples; multicast scope clamped to 239.0.0.0/8** (§7.6) — 2018 may have allowed IPv6 multicast and/or other scopes.

7. **`sip:` vs `sips:` URI form (§10.1.1)** — connection management, not SDP, but adjacent.

### AES3-specific observations

- AES3-1 and AES3-4 are entirely about wire-format and physical layer. **None** of the AES3 SHALLs directly constrain SDP grammar. They are the rationale for choices made downstream by AES67 / ST 2110-30 / ST 2110-31, but a parser implementing only AES3 wouldn't have any SDP rules to apply.
- AES3-1 §5.2 ("sampling frequency shall be in accordance with AES5") is *circumstantial evidence* for the AES67 / ST 2110-30 supported sample-rate set, not direct authority.
- AES3 has been amended since 2009 (notably AES3-2-2009 errata and various follow-on parts). The 2009 wording is stable enough that this is low-risk for SDP purposes, but the user should know.

### Important bullet-binding scopes captured

- AES67 §7.1 "When operating at 48 kHz sampling rate:" — bullets are constraints **scoped to 48 kHz operation**, not general rtpmap requirements. Same pattern for 96 kHz, 44.1 kHz. Capturing this avoids false-finding of "L16+L24 always required."
- AES67 §6.2 "Minimally the three traffic classes described in table 1 shall be supported." — bullet list is the table, not SDP content.
- AES3-4 §C.1.3 "The cable shall be one of the following types:" — three-item bullet list scopes to the cable-types clause, not the section.
- AES3-4 §C.4.1 "The pin usage shall be:" — Pin 1/2/3 bullets bind to the pin-usage clause.

### What an AES67 parser would actually need to enforce (synthesis, for the main thread)

For an SDP claiming AES67-2013 conformance:
- `m=audio … RTP/AVP <dynamic-PT>` with `a=rtpmap:<pt> L16/<rate>/<ch>` or `L24/<rate>/<ch>` where `<rate>` ∈ {44100, 48000, 96000} and `<ch>` ≥ 1 (warn if >8 because §7.3 says "may support more").
- `(rate, encoding)` combinations forbidden by §7.1 (e.g. L16 at 96 kHz is "outside the scope").
- `a=ptime:<value>` REQUIRED (§8.1); value must be a positive decimal.
- `a=maxptime:<value>` required only if multiple ptimes supported (cannot be enforced from a single SDP without offer/answer state).
- `a=ts-refclk:…` REQUIRED per stream (§8.2); for `ptp=IEEE1588-2008` the value must include `:<GMID>:<domain>`; for `ptp=IEEE802.1AS-2011` the value must NOT include a domain.
- `a=mediaclk:direct=<offset>` REQUIRED per stream (§8.3).
- If `c=IN IP4 <addr>` is multicast, `<addr>` must be in 239.0.0.0/8 (admin-scoped).

All of the above is **AES67-2013** wording. The main thread MUST re-verify against AES67-2018 (the version actually referenced by ST 2110-30:2025 §6.2.1) before encoding these as parse_sdp checks.

---

| 44 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 7.9 Derived Signals | shall | "then the sender shall determine the RTP Timestamps of the samples of the derived output signal as if it were a new signal \"sampled\" at the current time (TNEWRTP(j) = TNOW)" | Conditional RTP TS rule for time-resetting senders. | N | Wire behavior; conditional. |
| 45 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 7.9 Derived Signals | shall | "Senders which preserve the RTP timestamp values from their input to output as described in this section shall be referred to as time-preserving, while senders which create new RTP timestamps shall be referred to as time-resetting." | Definitional categorization. | N | Terminology, not a check. |
| 46 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 7.9 Derived Signals | shall | "In all cases, the \"regular increments\" requirements of section 7.6.1 or 7.7.1 shall take precedence over the behaviors described in this section." | Regular-increments rule takes precedence. | N | Wire behavior precedence. |
| 47 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.1 SDP General | shall | "Devices which contain one or more Senders shall construct one SDP session description as specified in IETF RFC 4566 for each RTP stream (or redundant pair of streams) that is originated by that device." | One SDP per RTP stream (or redundant pair). | Y | Defines unit of SDP description — one media or one redundant pair → one SDP. Important for DUP semantics. |
| 48 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.1 SDP General | shall | "These SDP objects shall be made available through a management API of the device." | SDP available via management API. | N | Device behavior, not SDP form. |
| 49 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.1 SDP General | shall | "Devices which contain one or more receivers shall provide a capability to ingest and act upon an SDP object created in accordance with the requirements of this standard." | Receivers shall ingest SDP. | N | Device capability. |
| 50 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.1 SDP General | shall | "These SDP objects shall be communicated through a management API of the device." | SDP communicated via management API. | N | Device behavior. |
| 51 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.2 ts-refclk Signaling | shall | "All stream descriptions shall have a ts-refclk attribute as specified in IETF RFC 7273 section 4." | Every stream description must have `a=ts-refclk`. | Y | SDP-checkable: presence of `a=ts-refclk` on every stream. RFC 7273 governs form. |
| 52 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.2 ts-refclk Signaling | shall | "Devices which are referenced to IEEE Std 1588-2008 shall use the ts-refclk:ptp form, signaling either the grandmaster clockIdentity and domain number, or signaling that the PTP is traceable." | PTP-locked devices must use `ts-refclk:ptp=...` form. | Y | SDP-checkable: form `a=ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE1588-2008:<clockid>:<domain>` OR `a=ts-refclk:ptp=IEEE1588-2008:traceable`. |
| 53 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.2 ts-refclk Signaling | shall (scope intro) | "Devices shall signal that the PTP is traceable in the SDP if the following conditions are all met:" — scope: intro clause introducing the bulleted condition list (all three bullets are device-state predicates, not SDP form rules). | Intro clause governing traceable signaling conditions. | N | Bullet-binding marker. Bullets ("PTP timescale in use", "timeTraceable indicates traceable", "clockAccuracy ≤ 250ns") are device state, not SDP form. |
| 54 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.2 ts-refclk Signaling | shall | "Devices which are not referenced to IEEE Std 1588-2008 shall use an appropriate ts-refclk format as specified in IETF RFC 7272 [sic; typo for RFC 7273] or the extended form shown below, indicating the MAC address of the Sender using the token localmac." | Non-PTP devices must use appropriate RFC 7273 form or extended `localmac=` form. | Y | SDP-checkable form. Note: spec says "IETF RFC 7272"—likely an editorial error for RFC 7273. AMBIGUOUS (RFC 7272 does not relate to ts-refclk). |
| 55 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.2 ts-refclk Signaling | defined value (form) | "a=ts-refclk:localmac=<Ethernet MAC address of sender>" | localmac form is `a=ts-refclk:localmac=<MAC>`. | Y | Defined-value form for the `localmac` token. SDP-checkable. |
| 56 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.3 mediaclk Signaling | shall | "All stream descriptions shall have a media-level mediaclk attribute as per IETF RFC 7273 section 5." | Every stream description must have media-level `a=mediaclk`. | Y | SDP-checkable: `a=mediaclk` at media level on every m= section. |
| 57 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.3 mediaclk Signaling | shall | "If the Media Clock is directly derived from the Timestamp Reference Clock, the direct reference shall be used and the offset shall be included." | When direct, must use `direct=` form WITH offset. | Y | SDP-checkable: `a=mediaclk:direct=<offset>` form, offset present. |
| 58 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.3 mediaclk Signaling | defined value (form) | "In this case, as per clause 7.3 of this document, the offset will be zero. For example: a=mediaclk:direct=0" | Offset value = 0 when `direct=` used. | Y | SDP-checkable: when `a=mediaclk:direct=N`, N must equal 0. Cross-refs §7.3. |
| 59 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.3 mediaclk Signaling | shall | "If the Media Clock is asynchronous with respect to the Timestamp Reference Clock, for example if the input media stream for a Sender is not locked to the Common Reference Clock, the following form shall be used: a=mediaclk:sender" | Async case must use `a=mediaclk:sender` form. | Y | SDP-checkable form for the async case. Defined-value: the literal `sender` token. |
| 60 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.5 Duplicate Stream Signaling | shall | "Senders which transmit these duplicated RTP streams, using the mechanisms of Separate Source Addresses (IETF RFC 7104, Section 4.1) or Separate Destination Addresses (IETF RFC 7104, section 4.2) shall signal the RTP duplication using the session level group attribute of IETF RFC 5888 and the duplication grouping DUP semantics of IETF RFC 7104." | Duplicated streams must use session-level `a=group:DUP` (RFC 5888 + 7104). | Y | SDP-checkable: presence and placement (session-level) of `a=group:DUP …`, with each tag matched by `a=mid:…` per RFC 5888/7104. |
| 61 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.5 Duplicate Stream Signaling | shall not | "Redundant streams shall not use both identical source addresses and identical destination addresses at the same time." | Redundant streams must differ in source or destination address. | Y | SDP-checkable: across the two m= sections in a DUP group, (src,dst) pair must differ in at least one coordinate. Source from `a=source-filter`/`c=`; destination from `c=`. |
| 62 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.6 UDP Datagram Size | shall | "Senders operating with UDP Sizes which exceed the Standard UDP Size Limit shall include a Format Specific Parameter MAXUDP with a decimal value indicating the largest UDP Datagram Size (in octets) that might be present in the stream." | MAXUDP fmtp param required when > Standard limit; value is decimal octets. | Y | SDP-checkable: when MAXUDP is present in fmtp it must be a decimal integer; receiver cannot independently verify the "if exceeds 1460" antecedent from SDP alone, but the value form is checkable. |
| 63 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.6 UDP Datagram Size | shall | "If the MAXUDP parameter is not present, Receivers shall assume the Standard UDP Size Limit specified in section 6.3." | Default = 1460 when MAXUDP absent. | N | Receiver semantics default. |
| 64 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.7 TSMODE / TSDELAY | shall | "If the TSMODE parameter is not present, the receiver shall presume a value of TSMODE=NEW." | Default TSMODE = NEW when absent. | N | Receiver default. |
| 65 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.7 TSMODE / TSDELAY | defined value set | "Allowed values are: TSMODE=SAMP … TSMODE=NEW … TSMODE=PRES …" | TSMODE legal values are exactly {SAMP, NEW, PRES}. | Y | SDP-checkable: when TSMODE present, value ∈ {SAMP, NEW, PRES}. |
| 66 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.7 TSMODE / TSDELAY | defined value (form) | "Format Specific Parameter TSDELAY is defined to signal the Transmission Delay DTX of senders as defined in section 0. The time value is represented as a decimal positive integer number of microseconds." | TSDELAY value is decimal positive integer (microseconds). | Y | SDP-checkable: when TSDELAY present, value matches `[0-9]+` (positive integer). Note: "positive integer" plus the Annex B example `TSDELAY=0` is internally inconsistent — strict reading of "positive" excludes 0. AMBIGUOUS. |
| 67 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.7 TSMODE / TSDELAY | shall | "If the TSDELAY parameter is not present, the receiver shall take a receiver-dependent action." | TSDELAY-absent default is receiver-dependent. | N | Receiver behavior, not SDP form. |
| 68 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.7 TSMODE / TSDELAY | shall | "Senders specified in section 7.9 as time-preserving, when acting upon input signals with a value of TSMODE=SAMP, shall include in their SDP the TSMODE parameter with a value of SAMP, and TSDELAY with a value representative of their inclusive transmission delay DTX in the SDP." | Time-preserving senders with SAMP input → must signal TSMODE=SAMP + TSDELAY. | Y | SDP-checkable form (presence + value), conditional on sender role and input — role is not observable from SDP, so cannot be strictly enforced as a receiver-side check. |
| 69 | ST 2110-10:2022 | 8.7 TSMODE / TSDELAY | shall | "In any other case, such a time-preserving sender shall include TSMODE=PRES and an appropriate TSDELAY value." | Time-preserving senders in any other case → TSMODE=PRES + TSDELAY. | Y | Same as #68: SDP-form rule, but role-conditional. |

**Totals**

- Total rows: **69**
- SDP-Y (potentially SDP-checkable, in scope for `parse_sdp`): **24** (rows 4, 5, 8, 11, 18, 20, 24, 42, 43, 47, 51, 52, 54, 55, 56, 57, 58, 59, 60, 61, 62, 65, 66, 68, 69 — count includes definitional cross-refs)
- AMBIGUOUS: **2** (row 54 — "RFC 7272" likely a typo for RFC 7273; row 66 — "positive integer" wording conflicts with Annex B `TSDELAY=0` example)
- AES67-2013 flag rows: **0** — ST 2110-10:2022 normatively references **AES67-2018** (line 195 of extract). The earlier 2013/2015 AES67 wording is not in play here.

**Observations**

- ST 2110-10:2022 is the SDP umbrella for the whole 2110 family. Of 69 normative rows, roughly a third describe SDP form constraints directly; the remainder are device capability, wire-format, or behavioral requirements that fall outside SDP-document validation per the project's strictness principle.
- **Hard SDP-form rules** (presence/form/defined-value) cluster in §8: ts-refclk presence and form (#51, #52, #54, #55); mediaclk presence and form (#56, #57, #58, #59); DUP group placement (#60); redundant-address distinctness (#61); MAXUDP value form (#62); TSMODE value set (#65); TSDELAY value form (#66); presence-dependency TSMODE=SAMP → TSDELAY (#43); §7.3 mediaclk offset = 0 (#24) cross-refs §8.3.
- **Cross-spec dependencies**: row 4 (proto=RTP/AVP) is the gate for all SDP transport-form checks; row 8 (PT 96–127) is a defined value set conditioned on the absence of a fixed PT designation — that carve-out matters when ST 2110-30 specifies certain audio formats with potentially different PT semantics; row 20 (RFC 5771 forbidden multicast blocks: 224.0.0.0/24 Local Network Control, 224.0.1.0/24 Internetwork Control) is SDP-observable via `c=` lines.
- **Bullet-binding traps avoided**: §7.6.4 has a bulleted list whose scope intro is "the RTP timestamps shall be determined as follows:" — the bullets are wire-format determinations, not SDP rules (rows 33–36). §8.2 has a bulleted list whose scope intro is "Devices shall signal that the PTP is traceable in the SDP if the following conditions are all met:" — the bullets describe device-state predicates (PTP timescale in use, timeTraceable=traceable, clockAccuracy ≤ 250ns), not SDP-form rules (row 53). Reading these bullets as SDP-validation requirements would be a false-finding trap.
- **§7.3 offset = 0** is a clean cross-clause constraint: the mediaclk form lives in §8.3, but the value rule is in §7.3. Parser should enforce it as a single check tied to either citation.
- **Editorial issue (row 54)**: spec body line 763 cites "IETF RFC 7272" where context strongly indicates RFC 7273 (the ts-refclk source RFC). Flagged AMBIGUOUS rather than resolved — primary text says 7272.
- **Editorial issue (row 66)**: TSDELAY is defined as "decimal positive integer" but Annex B (informative) shows `TSDELAY=0`. Strict reading of §8.7 excludes 0; Annex B is informative so cannot override. AMBIGUOUS. Recommend treating non-negative integer as the practical bound, but the conformance check should follow primary normative text.
- **Out-of-SDP-scope categories**: device control surface (#22), PTP message-rate support (#23), wire-format RTP timestamp determination (§7.5–§7.9, mostly), receiver-default semantics (#63, #64, #67). These are correctly out-of-scope for an SDP parser per the project's strictness principle ("RTCP-layer signaling … live in RTP / RTCP, not in SDP").

---

## SMPTE ST 2110-20:2022 (Uncompressed Active Video)

_Inventory file: `/tmp/audit_inventory_st2110-20.md`_

# Audit Inventory — SMPTE ST 2110-20:2022 (Uncompressed Active Video)

Source: `/Users/andrewstarks/Library/CloudStorage/Dropbox/Personal/Claude/Macnica/Standards Related/smpte_standards_internal/st2110-20-2022.md`

Conformance notation reminder (§2):
- "shall" / "shall not" = strict requirement / prohibition.
- "should" / "should not" = recommendation, not strict requirement.
- "may" / "need not" = permission.
- "reserved" = not defined now, shall not be used. "forbidden" = reserved + never to be defined.
- Bullets bind to their immediately introducing clause, never to the section header.

SDP? legend:
- Y = the clause constrains SDP content (a=rtpmap, a=fmtp, m=, etc.) directly observable in an SDP file.
- N = out-of-SDP scope (RTP packet wire format, traffic shaping, receiver behaviour, etc.).
- M = mixed; clause has both an SDP component and an out-of-SDP component — flagged in Notes.

| # | Spec | § | Verb | Verbatim quote | Summary | SDP? | Notes |
|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|---|
| 1 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §2 | shall (precedence) | "Unless otherwise specified, the order of precedence of the types of normative information in this document shall be as follows: Normative prose shall be the authoritative definition; Tables shall be next; then formal languages; then figures; and then any other language forms." | Source-precedence rule; meta-rule, not a stream check. | N | Meta-conformance; not a stream check. |
| 2 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.1 | shall | "The sample arrays of the active video essence shall be transported using RTP (IETF RFC 3550), subject to the constraints and payload definition below." | Active video MUST be transported using RTP. | N | RTP wire-format requirement; cannot be checked from SDP alone (the m=video line uses RTP/AVP, which is an SDP indicator, but the transport itself is wire-level). |
| 3 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.1 | shall | "Unless otherwise noted, multi-octet fields within the RTP Header, RTP Payload Header, and RTP Payload shall be transmitted in Network Byte Order (most significant byte first)." | RTP wire byte order. | N | Wire-format. |
| 4 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.1 | shall | "When represented in bit-field diagrams such as Figure 1 or Figure 2, the most significant bits of multi-bit fields shall occupy the lowest-numbered bit index positions (left-most positions in the figures), and shall be transmitted first." | Bit-ordering in diagrams and transmission. | N | Wire-format. |
| 5 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.1 | shall | "The image technical metadata necessary to receive and interpret the RTP stream shall be communicated via SDP as defined in section 7." | Image metadata MUST be communicated via SDP §7. | M | Establishes SDP as the only signalling channel; the §7 sub-clauses provide the concrete SDP checks. |
| 6 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.1 | shall | "Traffic shaping and transmission timing of the RTP stream shall be in accordance with the Network Compatibility Model compliance definitions specified in SMPTE ST 2110-21 for Narrow Senders (Type N), Narrow Linear Senders (Type NL), or Wide Senders (Type W)." | Sender traffic-shaping must follow ST 2110-21 Type N/NL/W. | N | Traffic shaping is signalled via TP fmtp parameter in ST 2110-21, not in ST 2110-20 fmtp. |
| 7 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.1 | shall | "Where the Media Clock is locked to the timestamping reference clock, traffic shaping and delivery timing shall also be in accordance with the Virtual Receiver Buffer Model compliance definitions specified in SMPTE ST 2110-21 for Narrow Senders (Type N), Narrow Linear Senders (Type NL), or Wide Senders (Type W)." | VRX delivery timing per ST 2110-21. | N | Out-of-SDP timing behaviour. |
| 8 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.1 | shall | "Receivers shall conform to one of the types specified in ST 2110-21:2022 section 7.2." | Receiver-type conformance. | N | Receiver behaviour, not SDP content. |
| 9 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.2 | shall | "The fields of the RTP packet header and their order shall be as defined in IETF RFC 3550." | RTP header field order. | N | Wire-format. |
| 10 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.2 | shall | "The Payload Type field shall refer to the dynamically allocated payload type as specified in SMPTE ST 2110-10 section 6.2 'Real-Time Transport Protocol (RTP)'." | PT shall be dynamic. | M | The actual PT value appears in the SDP m= line and a=rtpmap; ST 2110-10 §6.2 also defines this. Implication: the PT in SDP must be in the dynamic range (96–127). Primary SDP-relevant constraint is owned by ST 2110-10. |
| 11 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.2 | shall | "The Timestamp field shall contain the RTP Timestamp as specified in SMPTE ST 2110-10." | RTP timestamp per ST 2110-10. | N | Wire-format. |
| 12 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.2 | shall | "The SSRC field shall be as specified in IETF RFC 3550" | SSRC per RFC 3550. | N | Wire-format. |
| 13 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.2 | shall | "For progressive scan video, the marker bit shall be set to 1 to denote when this RTP packet is the last packet carrying video essence data for a video frame, and set to 0 for all other packets." | Marker bit semantics (progressive). | N | Wire-format. |
| 14 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.2 | shall | "For interlaced video, the marker bit shall be set to 1 to denote when this RTP packet is the last packet carrying video essence data for a video field, and set to 0 for all other packets." | Marker bit semantics (interlaced). | N | Wire-format. |
| 15 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.2 | shall | "The RTP header sequence number field shall contain the 16 low order bits of the extended 32-bit RTP packet sequence counter." | Seq number = low 16 bits of extended seq. | N | Wire-format. |
| 16 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.2 | shall (cond.) | "When this bit is set, an RTP header extension is present immediately following the SSRC field. If present, the header extension shall be compliant to IETF RFC 8285." | If X-bit, ext is RFC 8285. | N | Wire-format. |
| 17 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.3 | shall | "The Media Clock, RTP Clock, and RTP Timestamps shall comply with the provisions of SMPTE ST 2110-10." | Clock provisions per ST 2110-10. | N | Cross-document; timing rules. |
| 18 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.3 | shall | "The RTP Clock rate for streams compliant to this standard shall be 90 kHz." | RTP clock rate = 90 kHz. | Y | SDP a=rtpmap rate field MUST be 90000 for raw video (RFC 4566 a=rtpmap:<pt> raw/90000). See also §7.1 row #50. |
| 19 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.3 | shall | "All RTP packets which are part of the same progressive frame shall contain the same RTP Timestamp value." | Same RTP timestamp per progressive frame. | N | Wire-format. |
| 20 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.3 | shall | "All RTP packets which are part of the same interlaced field shall contain the same RTP Timestamp value." | Same RTP timestamp per interlaced field. | N | Wire-format. |
| 21 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "The RTP Payload Header shall include the Extended Sequence Number, followed by one, two, or three Sample Row Data (SRD) Headers." | Payload header composition. | N | Wire-format. |
| 22 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "The Extended Sequence Number field shall contain the 16 high order bits of the extended 32-bit sequence number." | Extended-seq semantics. | N | Wire-format. |
| 23 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "The SRD Length field shall indicate the number of octets of data included from the indicated sample row, and shall be a multiple of the pgroup octet length." | SRD Length = octets, multiple of pgroup size. | N | Wire-format. |
| 24 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall be forbidden | "An SRD length of zero shall be forbidden except in the case where there is exactly one SRD Header – in which case the SRD length of zero indicates that no sample row data follows this header." | SRD Length=0 only allowed with single SRD header. | N | Wire-format. |
| 25 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "The Field Identification bit shall be set to 0 to signal data in the (temporally) first field and set to 1 to signal data in the second field." | F-bit values. | N | Wire-format. |
| 26 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "For progressive scan data the Field Identification bit shall be set to zero, except in the case of Progressive segmented Frame (PsF) data, in which case the F bit indicates the segment." | F-bit for progressive/PsF. | N | Wire-format. |
| 27 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "The SRD Row Number field shall refer to Sample Row Numbers within the Sample Array, and shall start at 0 at the top of the transmitted image." | SRD Row Number semantics. | N | Wire-format. |
| 28 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "In the case of interlaced images, each field shall start at 0 at the top of the field." | SRD Row Number reset per field. | N | Wire-format. |
| 29 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "In the case of Progressive segmented Frame (PsF) data, the sample row numbering shall start at 0 at the top of each segment." | SRD Row Number reset per PsF segment. | N | Wire-format. |
| 30 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "SRD Row Number shall only increase within the field or frame (sample rows are sent in order from top to bottom)." | Monotonic SRD Row Number. | N | Wire-format. |
| 31 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "The Continuation bit shall be set to 1 if an additional Sample Row Data Header follows the current Sample Row Data Header in the RTP Payload Header, which signals that the RTP packet is carrying data for more than one sample row. The Continuation bit shall be set to 0 otherwise." | C-bit semantics. | N | Wire-format. |
| 32 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.4 | shall | "The SRD Offset field shall contain the horizontal position, within the full-bandwidth image pixel matrix, of the first full-bandwidth sample in the associated Sample Row Data Segment, where a value of 0 corresponds to the pixel at the left edge of the image." | SRD Offset semantics. | N | Wire-format. |
| 33 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall | "For 4:2:0 Sampling System with progressive video, the SRD Row Number shall be set to the first Sample Row of the pair of grouped sample rows. Only every other Sample Row shall be signaled in the SRD Row Number field." | 4:2:0 row-pair signalling. | N | Wire-format. |
| 34 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall | "SRD Offset shall only increase within the same sample row (samples are sent in order from left to right across the row)." | Monotonic SRD Offset within row. | N | Wire-format. |
| 35 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall | "The fields of an interlaced image shall be transmitted in time order, first field first." | Interlaced field tx order. | N | Wire-format. |
| 36 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall | "For interlaced systems and Progressive segmented Frame (PsF) systems, if the height is even, then the lines shall be divided evenly between the fields (or segments), and if the height is odd, the temporally first field (or segment) shall contain one more line than the temporally second field." | Even/odd line division between fields. | N | Wire-format / segmenting rule. |
| 37 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall not | "In progressive systems, a single RTP packet shall not contain samples from more than one frame." | One frame per packet (progressive). | N | Wire-format. |
| 38 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall not | "In interlaced systems, a single RTP packet shall not contain samples from more than one field." | One field per packet (interlaced). | N | Wire-format. |
| 39 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall not | "In Progressive segmented Frame (PsF) systems, a single RTP packet shall not contain samples from more than one segment." | One segment per packet (PsF). | N | Wire-format. |
| 40 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall | "In interlaced systems, for the purposes of image reconstruction, the sample rows of the temporally second field shall be displaced vertically 'below' the like-numbered sample rows of the temporally first field." | Field spatial reconstruction. | N | Receiver behaviour. |
| 41 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.1.5 | shall | "Similarly, in Progressive segmented Frame (PsF) systems, the sample rows of the second segment shall correspond to spatial locations below the like-numbered sample rows of the first segment." | Segment spatial reconstruction. | N | Receiver behaviour. |
| 42 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.1 | shall | "The Sample Row Data Headers shall be followed by Sample Row Data Segments, except in the special case where there is exactly one Sample Row Data Header and it indicates an SRD Length of zero." | SRD Header → Segment pairing. | N | Wire-format. |
| 43 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.1 | shall | "The order of the Sample Row Data Segments in the RTP payload shall correspond to the order of the Sample Row Data Headers that precede them." | Header/segment ordering. | N | Wire-format. |
| 44 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.1 | shall | "For each Sample Row Data Header, there shall be a Sample Row Data Segment in the payload (with the exception of the special case noted above)." | Header-segment 1:1. | N | Wire-format. |
| 45 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.1 | shall not | "RTP Packets shall not contain more than three Sample Row Data Headers." | Max 3 SRD headers per packet. | N | Wire-format. |
| 46 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.1 | shall | "Each Sample Row Data Segment shall include data from either a complete sample row, or a portion of a sample row." | Segment is whole or partial row. | N | Wire-format. |
| 47 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.1 | shall | "The length of each Sample Row Data Segment shall in all cases be an integer multiple of the pgroup size in octets." | Segment length multiple of pgroup. | N | Wire-format. |
| 48 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.1 | shall not | "The UDP size of each RTP packet shall not be larger than the prevailing UDP Size Limit (Standard or Extended) as defined in SMPTE ST 2110-10." | UDP size capped per ST 2110-10. | M | Limit is set by MAXUDP fmtp (§7.3) which IS in SDP; the packet-size check itself is wire-level. The SDP-visible part: MAXUDP value must be one of the legal limits — see ST 2110-10 for the closed set. |
| 49 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.1 | shall | "In such situations, the sender shall fill the remaining sample positions of the final pgroup with zero and the receiver shall ignore the fill data. The Length value in the Sample Row Data Header shall include this fill data." | Fill behaviour for final pgroup. | N | Wire-format. |
| 50 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.2 | shall (defined value) | "Every pgroup shall consist of an integer number of octets." | Pgroup octet boundary. | N | Wire-format consequence; the per-(sampling,depth) pgroup sizes are tabulated and reachable from SDP, but the constraint itself is wire-level. |
| 51 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.2 | shall not | "Pgroups shall not be fragmented across packets and shall not represent samples from more than one image source array line (or two source array lines in the case of 4:2:0 sampling)." | No-fragment / single-line (or pair) pgroups. | N | Wire-format. |
| 52 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.2 | shall | "The definition of which samples are represented in the pgroup shall be determined by the SDP parameters (as detailed in section 7)." | SDP parameters define pgroup composition. | M | Establishes SDP authority over pgroup composition. Concrete SDP-observable checks live in §7. |
| 53 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.2 | shall | "If color subsampling is used, sub-samples shall only be shared within the pgroup." | Sub-sample sharing scope. | N | Wire-format. |
| 54 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.3 | shall (table) | "When using the 4:4:4 sampling system, pgroups shall be constructed as described in Table 1." | 4:4:4 pgroup construction per Table 1. | M | Table 1 defines the closed value set for `(sampling, depth)` 4:4:4 combinations and their pgroup sizes. SDP-relevant: only the (sampling,depth) pairs listed are legal under this clause — see Table 1 for the matrix. AMBIGUOUS for SDP: whether 4:4:4 KEY appearing here at depths 8/10/12/16/16f is also constrained; KEY pgroups have their own Table 4. |
| 55 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.3 Table 1 | defined value set (sampling × depth, 4:4:4) | "YCbCr-4:4:4 / CLYCbCr-4:4:4 / ICtCp-4:4:4 / RGB / XYZ" with depths "8 / 10 / 12 / 16, 16f" except XYZ which lists "12 / 16, 16f" | 4:4:4 (sampling, depth) closed set. RGB family supports {8,10,12,16,16f}. XYZ supports {12,16,16f} (no 8 or 10 listed). YCbCr/CLYCbCr/ICtCp 4:4:4 support {8,10,12,16,16f}. | Y | scope: "When using the 4:4:4 sampling system, pgroups shall be constructed as described in Table 1." Therefore (sampling=XYZ, depth=8) and (sampling=XYZ, depth=10) are not defined and thus not legal SDP combinations under this standard. |
| 56 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.4 | shall (table) | "When using the 4:2:2 sampling system, pgroups shall be constructed as described in Table 2." | 4:2:2 pgroup construction per Table 2. | M | Table 2 defines the closed 4:2:2 (sampling, depth) set. |
| 57 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.4 Table 2 | defined value set (sampling × depth, 4:2:2) | "YCbCr-4:2:2 / CLYCbCr-4:2:2 / ICtCp-4:2:2" with depths "8 / 10 / 12 / 16, 16f" | 4:2:2 (sampling, depth) closed set: only YCbCr-4:2:2, CLYCbCr-4:2:2, ICtCp-4:2:2 sampling values exist with depths {8,10,12,16,16f}. | Y | scope: "When using the 4:2:2 sampling system, pgroups shall be constructed as described in Table 2." RGB-4:2:2, XYZ-4:2:2 etc are not defined, hence not legal under this standard. |
| 58 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.5 | shall | "The 4:2:0 sampling system shall only be applied to progressive scan images transmitted in a progressive manner." | 4:2:0 only for progressive (no PsF/interlaced). | Y | scope: clause introduces "This sampling system does not apply to PsF or interlaced video essence." A `sampling=YCbCr-4:2:0` (or `CLYCbCr-4:2:0` / `ICtCp-4:2:0`) combined with `interlace` (with or without `segmented`) is forbidden. Cross-parameter SDP check. |
| 59 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.5 | shall not (implied via "does not apply") | "This sampling system does not apply to PsF or interlaced video essence." | 4:2:0 forbidden for PsF / interlaced. | Y | scope: same as row 58. Note prose says "does not apply" — this is the explanatory restatement; the SHALL in the previous sentence is the binding text. |
| 60 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.5 | shall (table) | "When using the 4:2:0 sampling system, pgroups shall be constructed as described in Table 3 using the numbering illustrated in Figure 4." | 4:2:0 pgroup construction per Table 3. | M | Table 3 defines the closed 4:2:0 (sampling, depth) set. |
| 61 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.5 Table 3 | defined value set (sampling × depth, 4:2:0) | "YCbCr-4:2:0 / CLYCbCr-4:2:0" with depths "8 / 10 / 12"; "ICtCp-4:2:0" with depths "8 / 10 / 12" | 4:2:0 (sampling, depth) closed set: only YCbCr-4:2:0, CLYCbCr-4:2:0, ICtCp-4:2:0; depths {8, 10, 12} only — NO 16 and NO 16f. | Y | scope: "When using the 4:2:0 sampling system, pgroups shall be constructed as described in Table 3." Therefore (sampling=YCbCr-4:2:0, depth=16) or 16f etc. is not legal. |
| 62 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.5 | shall | "When packetizing progressive scan 4:2:0 Y'C'BC'R or ICTCP video data segments, samples from two consecutive luminance sample rows shall be included in each pgroup." | 4:2:0 paired-row packetization. | N | Wire-format. |
| 63 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.5 | shall | "The sample row number in the Sample Row Data Header shall be set to that of the first luminance sample row of the pair" | 4:2:0 SRD Row Number is first luma row of pair. | N | Wire-format. |
| 64 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.6 | shall | "The Key signal shall be as defined in SMPTE RP 157." | Key signal definition per RP 157. | N | Reference-only constraint; meaning of Key. |
| 65 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.6 | shall (table) | "The pgroups of the Key signal shall be constructed as described in Table 4." | Key pgroup per Table 4. | M | Table 4 defines key (sampling=KEY, depth) combinations. |
| 66 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.2.6 Table 4 | defined value set (Key sampling × depth) | "Key" with depths "8 / 10 / 12 / 16, 16f" | KEY sampling allowed at depths {8,10,12,16,16f}. | Y | scope: "The pgroups of the Key signal shall be constructed as described in Table 4." When sampling=KEY (capitalized "KEY" per §7.4.1), depth MUST be in {8,10,12,16,16f}. |
| 67 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.1 | shall | "Senders conforming to this standard shall operate in one of these packing modes, and shall signal their mode through the use of the appropriate Media Type parameter as indicated." | Senders MUST signal a packing mode via Media Type parameter. | Y | Requires fmtp `PM` parameter to be present. See §7.2 row #88 for the PM requirement; cross-cite to §6.3.2 and §6.3.3 for the two legal values. |
| 68 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.1 | shall | "Receivers compliant to this standard shall be capable of receiving all of the listed packing modes." | Receivers must accept both PM values. | N | Receiver capability, not SDP content. |
| 69 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.2 | shall | "Senders compliant to this packing mode shall signal compliance with a PM Media Type Parameter with value 2110GPM." | GPM ⇒ PM=2110GPM. | Y | Defined value: `PM=2110GPM` when General Packing Mode is in use. |
| 70 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.3 | shall | "This mode is a constrained subset of the General Packing Mode (GPM) defined in section 6.3.2, such that the sum of the lengths of the Sample Row Data Segments shall be a multiple of 180 octets." | BPM segment-sum multiple of 180. | N | Wire-format. |
| 71 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.3 | shall | "The largest multiple of 180 consistent with the prevailing maximum UDP size limit shall be used." | BPM largest 180-multiple. | N | Wire-format. |
| 72 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.3 | shall | "When operating in this mode, the Line Continuation ('C') bit shall be used in order to pack samples from more than one sample row into the current packet, in order to maintain a consistent number of 180 octet blocks per packet." | BPM use of C bit. | N | Wire-format. |
| 73 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.3 | shall | "Accordingly, a payload of 7 x 180 octets per packet shall be used." | BPM 7×180 payload. | N | Wire-format. |
| 74 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.3 | shall not | "The last packet of a field or frame shall not be subject to the 180 octet multiple rule above, and may be either truncated or padded with zeros resulting in the same sized packet as those preceding it." | Last packet exempt from 180-rule. | N | Wire-format. |
| 75 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.3 | shall not | "The Extended UDP size limit defined in SMPTE ST 2110-10 shall not be used in the Block Packing Mode." | BPM forbids Extended UDP limit. | Y | scope: "shall not be used in the Block Packing Mode." Cross-parameter SDP check: if `PM=2110BPM`, then `MAXUDP` MUST NOT signal a value indicating the Extended UDP size limit. (Definition of which values mean Extended belongs to ST 2110-10; the prohibition lives here.) |
| 76 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §6.3.3 | shall | "Senders compliant to this mode shall signal compliance with a PM Media Type Parameter with value 2110BPM." | BPM ⇒ PM=2110BPM. | Y | Defined value: `PM=2110BPM` when Block Packing Mode is in use. Combined with §6.3.2 row #69: PM closed set = {2110GPM, 2110BPM}. |
| 77 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.1 | shall | "Senders and Receivers shall adhere to IETF RFC 4566 which describes how to map the Media Type Parameters below into the syntax of the SDP object." | SDP must conform to RFC 4566. | Y | SDP-level conformance. |
| 78 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.1 | shall | "The video streams described in this standard shall be declared in the SDP using the Media Type name video and the Media Subtype name raw." | m= media type "video", subtype "raw". | Y | `m=video ...` and `a=rtpmap:<pt> raw/...`. |
| 79 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.1 | shall | "The rtpmap clause of the SDP shall indicate the 90 kHz RTP Clock rate." | a=rtpmap clock rate = 90000. | Y | `a=rtpmap:<pt> raw/90000` mandatory. |
| 80 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.1 | shall | "The SDP metadata items below shall apply equally to all samples, rows, fields, and frames of a stream." | SDP applies uniformly to whole stream. | N | Interpretation rule; not directly checkable. |
| 81 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.1 | shall | "The <format specific parameters> section shall consist of a sequence of media type parameter entries, separated by the semicolon (';') character followed by whitespace." | fmtp params separated by `; ` (semicolon + whitespace). | Y | Defined value-form: fmtp inter-parameter separator is `;` followed by whitespace. Strict reading: a separator without whitespace would be non-conformant. Common practice files often use `; ` (single space); some use `;\r\n` (line folding) — both are "semicolon + whitespace". AMBIGUOUS edge: whether whitespace = exactly one space, or any RFC 4566 whitespace including line folding, is not specified here. |
| 82 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.1 | (negative statement, not "shall") | "There is no semicolon character after the last item." | No trailing semicolon in fmtp. | Y | The verb is "is", not "shall". Still a defined-value form constraint per §2 (all non-Note prose is normative by default). Strict: trailing `;` in fmtp is non-conformant. |
| 83 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.1 | shall | "The a=fmtp clause shall be terminated by a carriage return." | fmtp line ends with CR. | Y | Defined termination; RFC 4566 generally uses CRLF. Reading "carriage return" loosely here aligns with RFC 4566 line termination. AMBIGUOUS: whether "carriage return" means CR (0x0D) alone or CRLF as in RFC 4566 §5. RFC 4566 uses CRLF; this clause is consistent with that. |
| 84 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.1 | shall (bullet intro) | "Each media type parameter entry shall be constructed as either" — bulleted: "a <name>=<value> pair, with no whitespace within the name or value or between the name, equal sign, and value" / "a <name> standalone declaration, with no whitespace within the name." | fmtp entries are either `name=value` (no whitespace inside) or bare `name`. | Y | scope: "Each media type parameter entry shall be constructed as either:" — bullets bind to this intro. Defined value-form: every fmtp parameter is either `name=value` or `name` standalone (e.g. `interlace`, `segmented`). |
| 85 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.2 | shall (bullet intro) | "Senders shall include the following payload-format-specific Media Type parameters in the a=fmtp clause of the SDP for all streams conforming to this standard." | Required fmtp parameters list. | Y | scope: "Senders shall include the following payload-format-specific Media Type parameters in the a=fmtp clause of the SDP for all streams conforming to this standard." The required parameters listed under this intro: sampling, depth, width, height, exactframerate, colorimetry, PM, SSN. Each is a separate clause below. |
| 86 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.2 | shall (required + value-set) | "sampling — Signals the color difference signal sub-sampling structure. | 87 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.2 | shall (required + value-set) | "depth — Signals the number of bits per sample. | 88 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.2 | shall (required + value-set) | "width — Signals the number of pixels per row. Permitted values are integers between 1 and 32767 inclusive." | `width` required; integer in [1, 32767]. | Y | scope: §7.2 intro. Required. Defined range [1, 32767] inclusive. |

| 90 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.2 | shall (required + format) | "exactframerate — Signals the frame rate in frames per second. Integer frame rates shall be signaled as a single decimal number (e.g. '25') whilst non-integer frame rates shall be signaled as a ratio of two integer decimal numbers separated by a 'forward-slash' character (e.g. '30000/1001'), utilizing the numerically smallest numerator value possible." | `exactframerate` required; either integer decimal, or two integers separated by `/`, smallest numerator. | Y | scope: §7.2 intro. Required. Defined value-form: integer OR `num/den` with smallest numerator. AMBIGUOUS: "numerically smallest numerator value possible" implies reduced fraction; whether `60000/1001` is reduced (gcd-coprime) or merely "smallest among industry conventions". Strict read: must be reduced to lowest terms. |
| 91 | ST 2110-20:2022 | §7.2 | shall (required + value-set) | "colorimetry — Specifies the system colorimetry used by the image samples.
